{File:CL_RAD.txt  Index:18  Index Date:20120625  PL:66.67%  PS:33.33%  Trades:24  CL:2}

IF CLOSE OF 6 BARS AGO > CLOSE OF 7 BARS AGO
AND CLOSE OF 7 BARS AGO > CLOSE OF 3 DAYS AGO
AND CLOSE OF 3 BARS AGO > CLOSE OF 2 BARS AGO
AND CLOSE OF 2 BARS AGO > CLOSE OF 4 BARS AGO
THEN BUY NEXT BAR ON THE OPEN WITH
PROFIT TARGET AT ENTRY PRICE + 2.15 %
AND STOP LOSS AT ENTRY PRICE - 2.15 %
